### 11 con Bëatrice m'era suso in cielo

**gemini1-it**

| Italian | Lemma | English | Latin | Interlingua | French | Spanish | Portuguese | Romanian | Esperanto |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|

### 73 Ma perch' io non proceda troppo chiuso,

**gemini1-it**

| Italian | Lemma | English | Latin | Interlingua | French | Spanish | Portuguese | Romanian | Esperanto |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| Ma | ma | but | sed | sed | mais | pero | mas | dar | sed |
